<h3>\n     Angular md-color-picker\n    </h3>\n    <h5>\n     *** BETA ***\n    </h5>\n    <p style="margin-bottom: 5px;">\n     A pop up color chooser featuring:\n    </p>\n    <ul>\n     <li>\n      HSL Specturm\n     </li>\n     <li>\n      RGBA Sliders\n     </li>\n     <li>\n      Palette Selection\n     </li>\n     <li>\n      $cookie based history\n     </li>\n     <li>\n      Multiple output formats\n     </li>\n    </ul>\n    <h5>\n     Spectrum Selector\n    </h5>\n    <p>\n     Canvas based spectrum selection tool, no images or tricky css.\n    </p>\n    <h5>\n     RGBA Sliders\n    </h5>\n    <p>\n     Angular Material sliders and manual input.\n    </p>\n    <h5>\n     $cookie Based History\n    </h5>\n    <p>\n     If\n     <code>\n      $cookies\n     </code>\n     is not included in your app, the history function will fall back to an array based history that is reset on each reload.\n    </p>\n    <h5>\n     Multiple Output Formats\n    </h5>\n    <p>\n     Using\n     <a href="https://github.com/bgrins/TinyColor">\n      tinycolor.js\n     </a>\n     we can output hexadecimal, rgb(a), or hsl(a) formats.\n    </p>\n    <h5>\n     Misc.\n    </h5>\n    <ul>\n     <li>\n      Random Color on open (optional)\n     </li>\n     <li>\n      Input focus opens color chooser (optional)\n     </li>\n     <li>\n      Default color on open (optional)\n     </li>\n     <li>\n      Specify output type\n     </li>\n     <li>\n      Accepts label and icon for use in the generated\n      <code>\n       md-input-container\n      </code>\n     </li>\n    </ul>\n   </div>\n   <div class="layout-margin layout-column flex-40" flex="40" layout="column" layout-margin="">\n    <h2>\n     Demo\n    </h2>\n    <h4>\n     *** Text Color ***\n    </h4>\n    <p>\n     The text color field is not using the\n     <code>\n      openOnInput\n     </code>\n     attribute and you must click on the preview circle to open the color chooser.  This allows you to manually type a color value without opening the color chooser.\n    </p>\n    <p>\n     This field has a label and icon specified.\n    </p>\n    <h4>\n     *** Text Background ***\n    </h4>\n    <p>\n     The text background field is using the\n     <code>\n      openOnInput\n     </code>\n     and the\n     <code>\n      random\n     </code>\n     attributes.  This will maket he field open to a random color if one is not already selected when the input field receives focus.\n    </p>\n    <p>\n     This field only has the label specified.\n    </p>\n    <h4>\n     Text Style\n    </h4>\n    <md-input-container class="md-docs-dark-theme">\n     <label class="md-placeholder" for="select_1">\n      Font\n     </label>\n     <md-select
